Facilities: The hotel is not big as a whole, but it is very well planned. It has everything, including swimming pools, cinemas, restaurants, and playgrounds. The rooms will also be equipped with Lego and car pencil boxes that children like. Some parent-child rooms will also have different beds (children like it very much). Considering that there are children in the bathroom, there will be toilet seats for children.
Hygiene: I am a bit of a clean freak, so the first thing I do when I get to the room is to wipe every corner with alcohol wipes. It is obvious whether it is dirty or clean.
Environment: The hotel environment is relatively ordinary, with not much greenery. The last time I came, because there was no parking space, I parked behind the hotel. It was all under renovation and the dust was relatively large. The hotel has no special greenery and is an independent building.
Service: Service is really what I want to praise the most, because of service, many shortcomings can weaken it. This time, as soon as I entered the parking lot, the master saw me looking for a parking space and asked the temporary car next to me to give it to me. Thank you very much. After all, it is one to two. If the parking space is far away, it is really inconvenient to take things. After getting off the car, there will be a housekeeper to help with the luggage and check in. They will also help to take care of the children's activeness and running. After checking in, I was added to a service group, where there will be a housekeeper belonging to your room number. You can consult in the group at any time if you have any questions, including the movies we want to watch and the time period, which can be arranged in advance. The playground is very large, and the children are sweating profusely. There will be someone who will hand over a towel to dry the children's hair and remind them not to catch a cold. The only flaw is the breakfast buffet. I have eaten breakfast, lunch, and dinner. The worst is breakfast. I don‚Äôt know if it‚Äôs because breakfast is included in the room rate. I slacked off? When comparing the three meals, the difference is so big that it is inevitable to feel disappointed.

If the service of Taste of Suzhou Restaurant is excluded, 5 points can be given for service. But for guests, the hotel is a whole.

The hotel has ground and underground parking lots with ample parking spaces. The breakfast variety is relatively rich, you can try the special Aozao noodles, and there are also many varieties of Jiangsu and Zhejiang specialty snacks.
I need to talk about Taste Suzhou Restaurant. Because we had to order a New Year's Eve dinner, we ordered a set meal and reserved seats on New Year's Eve. Originally, I said that I could choose snacks, such as wontons and glutinous rice balls, but after all, the ritual of New Year's Eve still needs to be paid attention to. However, there were no snacks during the meal, and the pre-ordered set meal was served slowly. Because I have traveled out of town many times to celebrate the New Year, it is understandable that there are few staff and the waiting time is a little longer, but the difficulty of preparing the set meals has obviously become less difficult. There are not enough service staff. The restaurant manager criticizes an older waitress from time to time. He hopes that the manager can look at his cold face and understand the cold language. No snacks, no explanation, not even hot drinks, the excuse being that the hot drink machine was broken. Not wanting to spoil the mood, my husband communicated with the front desk after dinner.
